            // ensures js doesn't die if ads service fails.  
            // Note that we need to define the js here, since ad js is being rendered inline after this.
            (function(f) {
                // Fallback javascript, when the ad Service call fails.  
                
                if((window.csm === undefined || window.generic === undefined || window.consoleLog === undefined)) {
                    if (console !== undefined && console.log !== undefined) {
                        console.log("one or more of window.csm, window.generic or window.consoleLog has been stubbed...");
                    }
                }
                
                window.csm = window.csm || { measure:f, record:f, duration:f, listen:f, metrics:{} };
                window.generic = window.generic || { monitoring: { start_timing: f, stop_timing: f } };
                window.consoleLog = window.consoleLog || f;
            })(function() {});

<h1 class="header"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="name">Marvel's The Avengers 2: Age of Ultron</span>
<span class="nobr">(<a href="/year/2015/?ref_=tt_ov_inf">2015</a>)</span>
<br/><span class="title-extra" itemprop="name">
            "Avengers: Age of Ultron"
            <i>(original title)</i>
</span>
</h1>
<div class="infobar">
<time datetime="PT160M" itemprop="duration">
                160 min
</time>
                -
<a href="/genre/Action?ref_=tt_ov_inf"><span class="itemprop" itemprop="genre">Action</span></a>
<span class="ghost">|</span>
<a href="/genre/Adventure?ref_=tt_ov_inf"><span class="itemprop" itemprop="genre">Adventure</span></a>
<span class="ghost">|</span>
<a href="/genre/Fantasy?ref_=tt_ov_inf"><span class="itemprop" itemprop="genre">Fantasy</span></a>
                -
            <span class="nobr">
<a href="/title/tt2395427/releaseinfo?ref_=tt_ov_inf+" title="See all release dates"> 23 April 2015<meta content="2015-04-23" itemprop="datePublished"/>
(Germany)
</a> </span>
</div>
<div class="star-box giga-star">
<div class="star-box-rating-widget">
<div class="rating rating-list">
<div class="rating-ineligible">
<a href="/help/show_leaf?votestopfaq&amp;ref_=tt_ov_rt">Not yet released</a>

<div class="star-box-details" itemprop="aggregateRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/AggregateRating">
            (voting begins after release)
 
    </div>
<div class="clear"></div>
</div>
<p></p>
<p itemprop="description">
When Tony Stark tries to jumpstart a dormant peacekeeping program, things go awry and it is up to the Avengers to stop the villainous Ultron from enacting his terrible plans.</p>
<p></p>
<div class="txt-block" itemprop="director" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<a href="/name/nm0923736/?ref_=tt_ov_dr" itemprop="url"><span class="itemprop" itemprop="name">Joss Whedon</span></a>

    </div>
<div class="txt-block" itemprop="actors" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
<h4 class="inline">Stars:</h4>

<a href="/name/nm0262635/?ref_=tt_ov_st" itemprop="url"><span class="itemprop" itemprop="name">Chris Evans</span></a>, 
<a href="/name/nm0749263/?ref_=tt_ov_st" itemprop="url"><span class="itemprop" itemprop="name">Mark Ruffalo</span></a> <span class="ghost">|</span>

<h2>Storyline</h2>
<div class="inline canwrap" itemprop="description">
<p>
When Tony Stark tries to jumpstart a dormant peacekeeping program, things go awry and Earth's Mightiest Heroes, including Iron Man, Captain America, Thor, The Incredible Hulk, Black Widow and Hawkeye, are put to the ultimate test as the fate of the planet hangs in the balance. As the villainous Ultron emerges, it is up to The Avengers to stop him from enacting his terrible plans, and soon uneasy alliances and unexpected action pave the way for a global adventure.                <em class="nobr">Written by
<a href="/search/title?plot_author=Marvel+Studios&amp;view=simple&amp;sort=alpha&amp;ref_=tt_stry_pl">Marvel Studios</a></em> </p>
</div>
<span class="see-more inline">
<a href="/title/tt2395427/plotsummary?ref_=tt_stry_pl">Plot Summary</a>
<span>|</span>

</span>

<h2>Did You Know?</h2>
<div class="txt-block" id="trivia">
<h4>Trivia</h4>


When <a href="/name/nm0647634?ref_=tt_trv_trv">Elizabeth Olsen</a> and <a href="/name/nm1093951?ref_=tt_trv_trv">Aaron Taylor-Johnson</a> learned that their roles Wanda and Pietro Maximoff would be based on their "Marvel Ultimates" version, both actors read and studied every single issue in order to prepare for the role.        <a class="nobr" href="trivia?ref_=tt_trv_trv">See more</a>  
    </div>
<hr/>
<div class="text-block" id="quotes">
<h4>Quotes</h4>

[<span class="fine">to the Avengers</span>]
I know you're good people. I know you mean well. But you just didn't think it through. There is only one path to peace... your extermination.
